---
layout: "post"
title: "Simple Typed Lambda Calculus"
date: "2018-08-17"
categories: type-theory
toc: true
agda: true
latex: true
---

We present a formalisation of the syntax in Agda for the *Simple Typed Lambda
Calculus (STLC)* with some of its properties and the description of the
type-checking for this type system. We refactor the implementation by
[@gergoerdi](https://github.com/gergoerdi/stlc-agda/) for this calculus,
in particular the [Scopecheck](https://github.com/jonaprieto/stlctalk/blob/master/src/Scopecheck.agda)
and [Typecheck](https://github.com/jonaprieto/stlctalk/blob/master/src/Typecheck.agda) module.

The following source code tested with:

- Agda v2.5.4
- Agda Standard Library v0.16

The original content was firstly exposed here:

  - **Direct PDF file**: [EAFIT Logic seminar](https://github.com/jonaprieto/stlctalk/raw/master/slides/slides.pdf)
  - [https://github.com/jonaprieto/stlctalk](https://github.com/jonaprieto/stlctalk).



{: .foldable }

### Bound

Lambda terms using De Bruijn indexes.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="2034" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="Bound"></a><a id="2041" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#2041" class="Module">Bound</a> <a id="2047" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="2048" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#2048" class="Bound">Type</a> <a id="2053" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="2055" class="PrimitiveType">Set</a><a id="2058" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="2060" class="Keyword">where</a>

      <a id="3178" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="3180" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#3098" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="3182" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#2731" class="Datatype Operator">⊢</a> <a id="3184" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#1479" class="InductiveConstructor">lam</a> <a id="3188" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="3189" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#3087" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="3191" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#1399" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">∶</a> <a id="3193" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#3089" class="Bound">A</a><a id="3194" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="3196" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#3091" class="Bound">t</a> <a id="3198" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#2731" class="Datatype Operator">⇝</a> <a id="3200" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#2418" class="InductiveConstructor">lam</a> <a id="3204" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#3089" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="3206" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#3093" class="Bound">t&#39;</a>

### Scopecheck

Check representation of λ-terms using de Bruijn indexes.
Get a λ-term using de Bruijn indexes by given a λ-term with names.

{: .foldable }
<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="4263" class="Comment">-- ∃-syntax and ∄-syntax</a>

    <a id="5885" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="5887" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="5888" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#5888" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="5890" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="5892" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#2588" class="Function">Binder</a> <a id="5899" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#5878" class="Bound">n</a><a id="5900" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="5902" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="5904" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="5905" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#5905" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="5907" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="5909" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#1309" class="Function">Name</a><a id="5913" class="Symbol">)</a>
    <a id="5919" class="Comment">------------------------------</a>
    <a id="5954" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="5956" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Relation.Nullary.html#534" class="Datatype">Dec</a> <a id="5960" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="5961" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#4406" class="Function">∃[</a> <a id="5964" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#5964" class="Bound">t</a> <a id="5966" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#4406" class="Function">]</a> <a id="5968" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="5969" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#5888" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="5971" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#2731" class="Datatype Operator">⊢</a> <a id="5973" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#1455" class="InductiveConstructor">var</a> <a id="5977" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#5905" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="5979" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#2731" class="Datatype Operator">⇝</a> <a id="5981" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#5964" class="Bound">t</a><a id="5982" class="Symbol">))</a>

              <a id="6676" class="Keyword">with</a> <a id="6681" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#5264" class="Function">name-dec</a> <a id="6690" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#6650" class="Bound">Γ,y⊢varx⇝t</a>
            <a id="6713" class="Symbol">...</a>  <a id="6718" class="Symbol">|</a> <a id="6720" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Data.Sum.Base.html#470" class="InductiveConstructor">inj₁</a> <a id="6725" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#6725" class="Bound">x≡y</a>                    <a id="6748" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="6750" class="Bound">x≢y</a> <a id="6754" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#6725" class="Bound">x≡y</a>
            <a id="6770" class="Symbol">...</a>  <a id="6775" class="Symbol">|</a> <a id="6777" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Data.Sum.Base.html#495" class="InductiveConstructor">inj₂</a> <a id="6782" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#6782" class="Bound">p</a><a id="6783" class="Symbol">@(</a><a id="6785" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#6785" class="Bound">t′</a> <a id="6788" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#139" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">-by-</a> <a id="6793" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#6793" class="Bound">Γ⊢varx⇝t′</a><a id="6802" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="6804" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="6806" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#6534" class="Bound">∄t⟨Γ⊢varx⇝t⟩</a> <a id="6819" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#6782" class="Bound">p</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

We want to determine if given a variable context and a term,
it is possible to find its encoding using De Bruijn indexes.
If so, we got its respective construction for that lambda term.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="Scopecheck.check"></a><a id="7035" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#7035" class="Function">check</a>
    <a id="7045" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="7047" class="Symbol">∀</a> <a id="7049" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="7050" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#7050" class="Bound">n</a><a id="7051" class="Symbol">}</a>
    <a id="7057" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="7059" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="7060" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#7060" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="7062" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="7064" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#2588" class="Function">Binder</a> <a id="7071" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#7050" class="Bound">n</a><a id="7072" class="Symbol">)</a>
    <a id="7078" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="7080" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="7081" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#7081" class="Bound">t</a> <a id="7083" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="7085" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#1434" class="Datatype">S.Expr</a><a id="7091" class="Symbol">)</a>
    <a id="7097" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="7099" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Relation.Nullary.html#534" class="Datatype">Dec</a> <a id="7103" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="7104" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#4406" class="Function">∃[</a> <a id="7107" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#7107" class="Bound">t′</a> <a id="7110" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#4406" class="Function">]</a> <a id="7112" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="7113" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#7060" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="7115" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#2731" class="Datatype Operator">⊢</a> <a id="7117" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#7081" class="Bound">t</a> <a id="7119" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#2731" class="Datatype Operator">⇝</a> <a id="7121" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#7107" class="Bound">t′</a><a id="7123" class="Symbol">))</a>

  <a id="7129" class="Comment">-- By induction on the term syntax.</a>

  <a id="8655" class="Comment">-- Go from a representation that uses Names to one that uses de Bruijn indices</a>
  <a id="Scopecheck.scope"></a><a id="8736" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#8736" class="Function">scope</a> <a id="8742" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="8744" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="8745" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#8745" class="Bound">t</a> <a id="8747" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="8749" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#1434" class="Datatype">S.Expr</a><a id="8755" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="8757" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="8759" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="8760" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#8760" class="Bound">p</a> <a id="8762" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="8764" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Relation.Nullary.Decidable.html#897" class="Function">True</a> <a id="8769" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="8770" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#7035" class="Function">check</a> <a id="8776" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Data.Vec.html#712" class="InductiveConstructor">[]</a> <a id="8779" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#8745" class="Bound">t</a><a id="8780" class="Symbol">)}</a> <a id="8783" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="8785" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#2363" class="Datatype">Expr</a> <a id="8790" class="Number">0</a>
  <a id="8794" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#8736" class="Function">scope</a> <a id="8800" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#8800" class="Bound">t</a> <a id="8802" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="8803" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#8803" class="Bound">p</a><a id="8804" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="8806" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="8808" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#155" class="Field">proj₁</a> <a id="8814" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="8815" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Relation.Nullary.Decidable.html#1055" class="Function">toWitness</a> <a id="8825" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#8803" class="Bound">p</a><a id="8826" class="Symbol">)</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

    <a id="10521" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#10457" class="Function">K</a> <a id="10523" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="10525" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#9926" class="InductiveConstructor">tLam</a> <a id="10530" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="10531" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#9926" class="InductiveConstructor">tLam</a> <a id="10536" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#9860" class="InductiveConstructor">tVar</a><a id="10540" class="Symbol">)</a>

    <a id="10547" class="Keyword">postulate</a>
      <a id="Typing.A"></a><a id="10563" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#10563" class="Postulate">A</a> <a id="10565" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="10567" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#9449" class="Datatype">Type</a>
      <a id="Typing.B"></a><a id="10578" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#10578" class="Postulate">B</a> <a id="10580" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="10582" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#9449" class="Datatype">Type</a>
      <a id="Typing.C"></a><a id="10593" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#10593" class="Postulate">C</a> <a id="10595" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="10597" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#9449" class="Datatype">Type</a>

    <a id="10607" class="Comment">-- S : [] ⊢ lam (A ↣ (B ↣ C))</a>
    <a id="10641" class="Comment">--              (lam (A ↣ B)</a>
    <a id="10674" class="Comment">--                   (lam A</a>
    <a id="10706" class="Comment">--                     ((var (# 2)) ∙ (var (# 0))) ∙ ((var (# 1)) ∙ (var (# 0))) ))</a>
    <a id="10794" class="Comment">--        ∶ (A ↣ (B ↣ C)) ↣ (A ↣ B) ↣ A ↣ C</a>
    <a id="10842" class="Comment">-- S = tLam (tLam ((tLam ({! tVar  !} ∙ {!   !})) ∙ ({! tVar  !} ∙ {!   !}))) --  tLam (tLam (tLam ((tVar ∙ tVar) ∙ (tVar ∙ tVar))))</a>{% endraw %}</pre>
